10-03-2021 03:28:46 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like ''			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'jiny auto'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_vykon-kw`,pm1.`mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,pm1.`mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,pm1.`mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_barva`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

10-03-2021 07:16:48 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_vykon`,pm1.`mauta_test`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_test' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_test`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_test' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_test`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID)

			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_test' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_test`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

10-03-2021 07:36:22 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_vykon`,pm1.`mauta_test`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_test' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_test`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'jiny-auto'

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_test' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_test`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_test' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_test`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_test' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_test`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'jiny-auto'

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

10-03-2021 09:10:13 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_vykon-kw`,pm1.`mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,pm1.`mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,pm1.`mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_barva`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title

10-03-2021 09:10:33 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

11-03-2021 09:59:33 row /wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Hyundaii30-1.jpg
11-03-2021 10:01:20 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`mauta_cena`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cena' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cena`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cena' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cena`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`

11-03-2021 11:05:51 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`mauta_cena`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cena' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cena`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cena' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cena`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

11-03-2021 12:11:04 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_vykon-kw`,pm1.`mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,pm1.`mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,pm1.`mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_barva`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_vykon-kw`,pm1.`mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,pm1.`mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,pm1.`mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_barva`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 82

		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_rok-vyroby` BETWEEN 2018 AND 2020 AND `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

11-03-2021 03:08:17 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`mauta_cena`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cena' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cena`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'jiny-auto'

11-03-2021 03:43:22 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_vykon-kw`,pm1.`mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,pm1.`mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,pm1.`mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,pm1.`mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,pm1.`mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,pm1.`mauta_druh-phm`,pm1.`mauta_pocet-sedadel`,pm1.`mauta_pohanena-naprava`,pm1.`mauta_barva`,pm1.`mauta_rok-vyroby`,pm1.`mauta_cenaden`,pm1.`mauta_znacka`,pm1.`mauta_automat`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE `mauta_cenaden` BETWEEN 0 AND 100

11-03-2021 03:43:35 queryitem 
		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`mauta_cena`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cena' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cena`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'jiny-auto'

		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_vykon-kw' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_vykon-kw`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_zdvihovy-objem-ccm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_objem-zavaz-prostoru-l`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_max-rychlost-km-h' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_max-rychlost-km-h`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_uzitecna-hmotnost-kg`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_spotreba-kombinovana-l-100-km`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_druh-phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_druh-phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pocet-sedadel' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pocet-sedadel`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_pohanena-naprava' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_pohanena-naprava`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_barva' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_barva`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_rok-vyroby' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_rok-vyroby`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cenaden' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cenaden`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_znacka' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_znacka`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_automat' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_automat`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'auto-29020-fiduc_09'

		SELECT post_title,post_name,post_content,pm1.`mauta_dvere`,pm1.`mauta_osob`,pm1.`mauta_karoserie`,pm1.`mauta_phm`,pm1.`mauta_cena`,pm1.`_thumbnail_id`  FROM
		(SELECT post_title,post_content,post_name 
			,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_dvere' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_dvere`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_osob' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_osob`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_karoserie' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_karoserie`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_phm' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_phm`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = 'mauta_cena' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `mauta_cena`,MAX(CASE WHEN pm1.meta_key = '_thumbnail_id' then pm1.meta_value ELSE NULL END) as `_thumbnail_id`
			FROM wp_posts LEFT JOIN wp_postmeta pm1 ON ( pm1.post_id = ID) 
			WHERE post_id=id 
			AND post_status like 'publish' 
			AND post_type like 'mauta2'			
			GROUP BY ID, post_title
			) AS pm1
			 WHERE post_name like 'jiny-auto'
